<li><b>1852</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:medium.html>-</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:john.html>John</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brown.html>Brown</a>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:rab.html>Rab</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:his.html>his</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:friends.html>Friends</a>".

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a> (2734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sniden</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">snīthan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snīþaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sneyt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cut.html>cut</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cut.html>cut</a></li>

***snob.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snob.html>snob</a> (14899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snob.html>snob</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Shortened <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">snorbaard</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> borrowing <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">snurbaard</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Snurrbaart</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Snurboart</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:west.html>West</a> Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schnurrbart</i>.
